    // perf: preload for dimensionScreensize images
    var displayValues = window.asBuyFlow.heroData.displayValues;

    if (displayValues) {
        // html from dimension which has img tags, once for each variant
        var html = displayValues.dimensionScreensize.variantOrder.reduce(function(acc, variant) {
            // concat all the html to pass to jquery
            return acc.concat(displayValues.dimensionScreensize[variant].image);
        }, '');

        var $imageHtmlString = jQuery(html);
        var $images = jQuery('img', $imageHtmlString);

        // loop over img tags and create new images which will cause preload
        $images.each(function() {
            var img = new Image();
            img.src = jQuery(this).attr('src');
        });
    }

    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {

            <script type="text/javascript">
            jQuery(document).ready(function() {
                window.step1ModularController = new as.Step1ModularController('body', {
                    questionSummary: "#question-summary",
                    collapsablePOButton: "button.as-purchaseoptions-collapsable"
                });

                    window.DeliveryDatesControllerFlex = new as.DeliveryDatesControllerFlex(document,{
                        deliveryDateContainerSelector : ".rs-step1modular-deliverycontainer",
                        deliveryModelObserver : window.step1ModularController.options.partNumberMap,
                        localityLookupUrl : "/shop/address/locality-lookup",
                        deliveryMessageUrl : "/shop/delivery-message",
                        geoLookupUrl : "/shop/address/geo-lookup",
                        omnitureData: [window.s.pageName, "Step 1"],
                        doSendLeadQuoteMetric: true,
                        hasLittleDude: true 
                    });


            });

            var loadDeferedImages = function () {
                window.removeEventListener('scroll', loadDeferedImages);
                var pxroValue = jQuery.cookie('pxro');

                jQuery('img[data-defer-src]').each(function() {
                    var el = jQuery(this);
                    var deferSrc = el.attr('data-defer-src');
                    var scaleParam = el.attr('data-defer-scaleparams2');

                    if (pxroValue === "2" && scaleParam && deferSrc.indexOf(scaleParam) === -1) {
                        var srcPre = deferSrc.slice(0, deferSrc.lastIndexOf('?') + 1);
                        deferSrc = srcPre + scaleParam;
                    }
                    el.attr('src', deferSrc).removeAttr('data-defer-src');
                });
            };
            window.addEventListener('scroll', loadDeferedImages);

            window.addEventListener('load', function() {
                loadDeferedImages();

                if(window.as.AnimateOnScroll) {
                    window.as.AnimateOnScroll.init();
                }
            });

            </script>

                                            aria-expanded="{{#question-0}}true{{/question-0}}{{^question-0}}false{{/question-0}}">
                                            <span class="as-accordion-title">
                                                What does “SIM-free” mean?
                                            </span>
                                            <span class="icon icon-plus as-accordion-plusicon"></span>
                                        </button>
                                    </h3>
                                </div>
                                <div 
                                    data-render="materializer" 
                                    data-uid="question-0" 
                                    id="question-0" 
                                    data-show-height="computed" 
                                    data-hide-height="0" 
                                    class="ase-materializer ase-materializer-show" 
                                    {(data-shown)}="question-0" 
                                    data-shown-init="true">
                                    <div class="as-accordion-content row">
                                        <div class="as-accordion-box-content column large-10 small-12">
                                                    “SIM-free” means your iPhone doesn’t ship with a carrier SIM card. The SIM-free iPhone sold on apple.com and at the Apple Store is unlocked. That means you’re free to use a SIM card from any carrier that provides service for iPhone.
                                        </div>
                                     </div>
                                </div>

                            <li class="as-accordion-item">

                                                Which capacity is right for me?
                                            </span>
                                            <span class="icon icon-plus as-accordion-plusicon"></span>
                                        </button>
                                    </h3>
                                </div>
                                <div 
                                    data-render="materializer" 
                                    data-uid="question-1" 
                                    id="question-1" 
                                    data-show-height="computed" 
                                    data-hide-height="0" 
                                    class="ase-materializer ase-materializer-show" 
                                    {(data-shown)}="question-1" 
                                    >
                                    <div class="as-accordion-content row">
                                        <div class="as-accordion-box-content column large-10 small-12">
                                                    iPhone 7 and iPhone 7 Plus come in two capacities: 32GB and 128GB. The term “GB“ stands for gigabytes. The more gigabytes you have, the more content you can store on your iPhone, such as apps, games, photos, HD videos, music, and movies. If you have a large music or photo library or lots of apps, it’s a good idea to consider an iPhone with a larger capacity. If you rarely download apps or you don’t take many photos or videos, an iPhone with a smaller capacity may be better for you.
                                        </div>

                                        <div class="as-accordion-box-content column large-10 small-12">
                                                    <p>If you completed the carrier activation steps for AT&amp;T, Sprint, or Verizon when you purchased your new iPhone online, it will arrive ready to use. Just turn it on and follow the onscreen instructions to set it up. If you chose to skip carrier activation at the time of purchase, you’ll need to insert an active SIM card or contact a carrier to set up an account.</p>
<p>If you selected an iPhone for T-Mobile, it will come with the appropriate nano-SIM, but you’ll need to contact T-Mobile or visit an Apple Store to activate your iPhone. If you selected the SIM-free iPhone, you’ll need to insert your own nano-SIM card or obtain one from the supported carrier of your choice and activate it in order to use your iPhone.</p>

    <li>Available space is less and varies due to many factors. A standard configuration uses approximately 10GB to 12GB of space (including iOS and&nbsp;preinstalled&nbsp;apps) depending on the model and settings. Preinstalled apps use about 4GB, and you can delete these apps and restore them.</li>
   <li>AppleCare+ provides coverage for up to two incidents of accidental damage from handling. AppleCare+ with Theft and Loss provides coverage for up to two incidents of accidental damage, theft, and loss. Each incident is subject to a service fee or deductible. Taxes may apply. AppleCare+ with Theft and Loss requires the Find My iPhone feature to be enabled on your device at the time it is lost or stolen. Disabling it will void all coverage of theft and loss. You are not required to purchase AppleCare+ with Theft and Loss to participate in the iPhone Upgrade Program.</li>
</ol>

Promotional iPhone&nbsp;XR and XS pricing is after trade-in of iPhone&nbsp;7&nbsp;Plus. You must be 18 years or older. In-store trade-in requires presentation of a valid, government-issued photo ID (local law may require saving this information). Additional terms from Apple or Apple’s trade-in partners may apply.</p>
    <p><sup>†</sup>Offer only available on presentation of a valid, government-issued photo ID (local law may require saving this information). Sales tax on the full value of a new iPhone and any applicable fees may be due at time of purchase. Value of your current device may be applied toward purchase of a new iPhone via an available carrier financing plan. Offer may not be available in all stores and not all devices are eligible for credit. To see if your device is eligible, please visit Apple’s <a href="http://reuserecycle.abbti.brightstarcorp.com" data-slot-name="footnotesText" data-feature-name="Astro Link" data-display-name="AOS: reuserecycle.abbti.brightstarcorp.com" target="_blank">approved partner</a>. Some stores may have additional requirements. You will be required to agree to the full terms and conditions available at the Apple Store. Online and in-store values may vary.</p>
